<user>110026986907431877065</user><rating>2< /rating><Gmap_id>0x80c2be012b26f031:0xd9949b06dded465b<//Gmap_id><Pics>None< /Pics>< Text>
I had multiple issues with Ian's Movers:

(TL;DR They scratched my floor during the move and refused to pay for repair or fix it.)

1. They did not tell us that their pricing was $117 per hour only if paid in cash - the day of, we were informed the day of the move that it was $127 per hour if paid via card.

2. The move itself was generally fine - they got the job done. They were careful to wrap the furniture nicely so it was protected. HOWEVER, they scratched the floor of my new apartment. While I was hanging around as they moved my stuff, I saw one mover drop a piece of furniture and say "Oh shoot!" After the chaos of the move, I examined the floor where it was dropped, and there was a scratch that couldn't be wiped away. There were additional scratches located on other parts of the floor.

3. I understand that accidents happen and damage can occur during a move. My biggest issue is what happened next. When I contacted the company about the scratches, I asked how it would be remedied. They insisted that the movers told them they did not scratch my floor. When I informed them that I was present and saw the scratch happen in the moment, they huffed and puffed and said they'd come back to me. They went radio silent until my boyfriend very firmly communicated to them days later that they needed to remedy the issue. Shortly after, they sent a handyman to look at the damage. The handyman attempted to wipe away the scratches, which could not be wiped away with water or chemicals. To add insult to injury, the handyman suggested that we simply tell our landlord that the scratches already existed when we moved in. We were offended that we were asked to lie, but also upset that this "solution" could result with us getting stuck with the bill upon moving out down the road. Despite emailing the company once more regarding the result of the handyman visit, I received no further communication from them. There has been no offer to fix or reimburse for the cost of repairing the scratched floor.<//Text>

<text>Stopped in on Saturday evening for dinner. Had a great experience. Tried the ribs, pulled pork, and the brisket. Ribs were tasty with just right flavor and a little stickiness to the glaze, just right. Pulled pork celebrates the pork. You can add sauce to your taste but it comes straight off of the smoker with just the rub and the bark. I love that they have nothing to hide, I want to taste the pork shoulder before I sauce it and this was wonderful. And the brisket... Outstanding! Would I like a bit more bark, Yes. Do I prefer a bit more spice, Yes. But if I want to please just me then I should cook it myself. These guys are making fantastic Q way up on the NorCal coast and they can hang with anything I have had in CA. This is not EXACTLY central TX bbq but we're not in central TX.

The creamy slaw was really good and would be welcome at any church picnic. The poppers are fun with a little something extra in the cream cheese. Definitely worth trying a few. AND... the deviled eggs are worth the drive all by themselves. Now I'm not saying we snuck in a bottle of bourbon and paired it with the porkbelly topped eggs. But if we had, I bet it would have been Out Of This World! ( okay, We did. )

So why only 4 stars? Well, I try to take these notes pretty seriously and the food and service were 5 star all the way. The seating and decor are plain and a little cafeteria like. Very clean and I look forward to returning when they have made a ton of money and can put a few dollars into sprucing the place up. Please don't hold that against them. This is a great place that I look forward to again the next time I am this far north.< /text></record></dataset><record>

< text>
I read some reviews on that other site (which I won't name) and everyone raved about their BBQ.  I had their smoked ribs, nothing to write home about, the meat didn't have the slight chewiness that I like with my  pork ribs, but it also wasn't fall off the bone good either.  The BBQ sauce it came with was pretty generic.  They said the sauce was spicy but no hint of heat any where.  I also got the Jalapeno poppers which was half a grilled jalapeno stuff with cream cheese and topped with bacon bits.  One was had heat while the other wasn't spicy at all.  I also tried the deviled egg topped with pork belly, the egg lacked season and the pork belly wasn't enough to give it the pop.  The service here is good and friendly, don't come too late because they start running out of stuff.< /text>

107135160095019803258<//user>
<time>1534734625815</time><response>None<//response>< Review>
We ordered a Tuna Sushi Burrito, Spicy Miso Ramen and Takoyaki.

Staff was very attentive and quick.

Tuna Sushi Burrito: Flavors and texture were on point. The rice was a thin layer but not too thin where it broke. The garlic chips and 2 sauces as a dip was a plus. We ordered a Super size and shared, still very large portion.

Spicy Miso Ramen: It was not very spicy, broth was good but nothing unique. The noodles were way too much, so much we barely got any broth. The noodles were also weird, not the right noodles used for Japanese ramen. They used Chinese egg noodles. They also give you only half a soft flavored egg. What a tease!

Takoyaki: Yummy! They had the right sauces and I love the Bonito flakes!<//Review>

<text>Based on all the reviews I was excited to try this place out. Interesting menu choices from sushi, ramen, udon, salads, and burgers. We got the ramen, fried chicken, the free gyoza (via yelp checkin), and a caterpillar roll. The best thing was the roll. The ramen was ok, but seemed to be lacking something. The broth felt overly fatty. Fried chicken was also ok. And the gyoza was ugh.

Right in the middle of our meal all the lights turned off. I thought we had a blackout for a moment when all of a sudden one of the waiters starts shaking a tambourine. Then party lights started flashing and the wait staff sang happy birthday to one of the customers. Once it was over all the lights came back on. Never seen such a show at any ramen place before.

The building looks like it was an old Taco Bell. Complete with drive-through. The parking is ok but you have to watch out for the drive-through cars. No wifi is offered here. From the outside the place seems a bit shady.

The staff was friendly, helpful, and attentive.< /text><Pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPBM76EmGBJEkJT_XlV4_tq_cwGrZ9kXx9VCRYG=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNGAWkgY_6s8WbA1q-NqLOwOtfZwPBAGRQnHe_G=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPSS_A69DY3U9e6jva5OCxdKqYg-Sh-9vUpB089=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPqklPgfTRvIGvHUOceQ4R8cSzFP1Csm8oeZMYo=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPZmdYipNzGXPrMdxYlPrQ_Ozc0e0mHfNGTmPGE=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNX6vVa-7RRFG58H1dcJHHnIHqvFS0g9qP4zHXF=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMlQxc59xorkwb0GPzZoNVt9Cyn5JaDIia6cInw=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /Pictures><response>None</response>< gmap_id>

I knew this was highly rated. But its an old drive thru building. So wasnt expecting that much.

Sushi is fresh, prefect temperature, and boy the thick cuts. Didnt look that great but tasted really good.  And the sashimi combo comes with real wasabi (frozen), not the chemical paste we normally get. That was impressive.

Ok rolls are a little on the chunky side. But good value for money.

<rate>4<//rate><user_id>118426146581985919560</user_id><Resp>None<//Resp>< review>
This is my go-to sushi restaurant. I stick with three items, although there are plenty other options. My top three choices are 1) Jalapeno bomb, 2) Salmon Burrito (warning, the large stands up to its name, and if you want to eat something else, do yourself a favor and order a mini), and 3) Crunch Asparagus. I often pair my meal with their $2 draft Sapporo that is so cold there are ice chips floating at the top. Be sure to do a Yelp check-in for a free starter, drink (non acholic), or ice cream. The staff is friendly, and most often attentive, but they're working on hiring more people, so this should soon be remedied. Last fun fact, they have a drive thru. Yep, a sushi joint where you don't even need to leave your car to order.</review>
